          <img alt="Training-two-ladies.jpg" class="ofc" sizes="400px" src="/media/2547/training-two-ladies.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=400&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132267747640000000" srcset="/media/2547/training-two-ladies.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=250&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132267747640000000 250w, /media/2547/training-two-ladies.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=300&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132267747640000000 300w, /media/2547/training-two-ladies.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=400&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132267747640000000 400w, /media/2547/training-two-ladies.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=450&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132267747640000000 450w"/>
         </div>
         <div class="card__content">
          <span class="card__meta">
           Find a course
          </span>
          <h2>
           Introduction to Children and Young People’s Mental Health
          </h2>
          <p>
           This interactive online workshop will help you understand mental health and learn practical ways of working with children experiencing distress.
          </p>
          <span class="button button--icon">
           <svg>
            <use xlink:href="#next-icon">
            </use>
           </svg>
          </span>
         </div>
        </a>
       </li>
       <li class="listing__item swiper-slide">
        <a class="card" href="/find-help/conditions/phobias/">
         <div class="card__image">
          <img alt="group-of-four-right-aligned-opt" class="ofc" sizes="400px" src="/media/3995/group-of-four-right-aligned-opt.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=400&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132424848130000000" srcset="/media/3995/group-of-four-right-aligned-opt.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=250&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132424848130000000 250w, /media/3995/group-of-four-right-aligned-opt.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=300&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132424848130000000 300w, /media/3995/group-of-four-right-aligned-opt.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=400&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132424848130000000 400w, /media/3995/group-of-four-right-aligned-opt.jpg?anchor=center&amp;mode=crop&amp;width=450&amp;quality=80&amp;rnd=132424848130000000 450w"/>
         </div>
         <div class="card__content">
          <span class="card__meta">
           Conditions
          </span>
          <h2>
           Phobias
          </h2>
          <p>
           A phobia is an extreme fear of an object, person, animal, activity, place, feeling or situation. If you are struggling with a phobia, you are not alone. With help, you can get better.
          </p>
          <span class="button button--icon">
           <svg>
            <use xlink:href="#next-icon">
            </use>
           </svg>
          </span>
         </div>
        </a>
       </li>

          <h2>
           Involving Young People in Improving Wellbeing Support and Services
          </h2>
          <p>
           Learn how meaningfully involving young people in wellbeing support and services can support a whole system approach to mental health.
